## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology (population dynamics / population growth ODEs)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is the time-derivative of population size P, which is the standard state variable in continuous-time population dynamics. Typical relationships encode density-independent growth (birthŌĆōdeath balance), density dependence (carrying capacity), Allee effects at low density, and time-varying/seasonally forced parameters via t.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Constant net influx/harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (immigration/emigration or stocking/constant removal approximation)
- Time-dependent intrinsic rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P (slow trend in environment affecting per-capita growth)
- Seasonally forced growth rate: dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * sin(c2 * t + c3)) * P (periodic environment/seasonality)
- Gompertz growth (ODE form): dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (multiplicative growth with log-density dependence)
- Generalized logistic / Richards model (ODE form): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (P / c1) ** c2) (flexible density dependence shape)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P ** (1 + c2) (crowding term as a higher-order power of P)
- Allee effect (strong Allee): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / c1) * (P / c2 - 1) (reduced growth at low density plus carrying capacity)
- Allee effect (smooth rational form): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) / (P + c2) (low-density inhibition with saturation of the Allee term)
- Harvesting (linear effort): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / c1) - c2 * P (proportional removal/fishing effort)
- Harvesting (saturating, Holling-type): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / c1) - c2 * P / (P + c3) (limited harvesting capacity at high P)
- Environmental carrying capacity trend: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / (c1 + c2 * t)) (time-varying carrying capacity)
- Catastrophe/pulse forcing (smooth approximation): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - P / c1) - c2 * exp(-c3 * (t - c4) ** 2) * P (transient shock reducing growth)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Per-capita growth rate form: if (dP_dt / P) is ~constant, use dP_dt = c * P; if it declines with P, model (dP_dt / P) as a decreasing function of P (e.g., linear in P, log(c/P), or power in P).
- Carrying capacity signatures: dP_dt crosses zero at a positive P and is positive below/negative above ŌåÆ include factors like (1 - P/c) or log(c/P).
- Skewed approach to equilibrium: slower-than-logistic near carrying capacity often fits Gompertz (log(c/P)) better than polynomial density dependence.
- Allee threshold behavior: negative growth at small P but positive at intermediate P implies an additional root at P Ōēł c (e.g., (P/c - 1) factor or (P - c)/(P + c)).
- Harvest/management detection: if dP_dt is systematically reduced roughly proportional to P, add a -c*P term; if removal rate saturates at high P, use -c*P/(P+c).
- Seasonality detection: periodic patterns in residuals vs t suggest using sin(c*t + phase) modulation of growth rate or carrying capacity.
- Regime shifts over time: monotonic drift in equilibrium level suggests allowing parameters like intrinsic rate or carrying capacity to depend on t (e.g., c0 + c1*t or c0/(c1 + c2*t) forms).
- Transient shocks: brief departures from typical dynamics localized in time suggest additive/multiplicative pulse terms in t (e.g., exp(-c*(t-t0)^2) acting on P).
